Roosevelt's Peace Speech

A Shot in the Arm for European Politics

Supporting the League of Nations, Opposing Military Expansion

Echoing French Policy

(Paris) The speech given yesterday by U.S. President Roosevelt has been enthusiastically received by the French, who widely believe that the United States is gradually broadening its interpretation of the Monroe Doctrine, as evident in Roosevelt's speech yesterday. On one hand, Roosevelt is supporting the League of Nations, and on the other hand, he is opposing the expansion of armaments and formally endorsing a permanent international system for monitoring armaments. This demonstrates that the United States is echoing France on various major international issues. Yesterday's meeting between U.S. Ambassador to Russia Bullitt and French Undersecretary of State Tedeschi further increases the satisfaction of French public opinion, as Bullitt is a close friend of President Roosevelt. French public opinion also believes that Roosevelt's speech will have a significant impact worldwide, especially in Berlin, at a time when Germany is demanding rearmament. As for London's wavering attitude and Rome's obvious opposition to the League of Nations, it is believed that Roosevelt's words will also have an impact on these two capitals. Journalist Blanc wrote in "Le Journal": "Roosevelt's speech is like a shot in the arm. How can we not express our admiration for Roosevelt? At a time when the United States is facing many domestic challenges and those bearing national responsibilities face numerous difficulties, Roosevelt is still able to make such an important statement on the international stage, which is truly admirable. Moreover, the failure of former Democratic President Wilson was precisely due to the Senate's opposition to his foreign policy. Roosevelt dared to challenge the Senate on the anniversary of Wilson's death, demonstrating exceptional courage." (Agence Havas, 29th)

Supplement to Roosevelt's Speech

(Washington) President Roosevelt delivered a speech yesterday at the Board of Directors of the "Wilson Foundation," as reported by this agency yesterday. Additional details of the unmentioned content of the previous dispatch are provided below. President Roosevelt reiterated his previous proposals on disarmament and renouncing aggression.

Support for the Monitoring System (1) All countries should gradually abandon offensive weapons within a certain number of years and no longer manufacture them but have the right to strengthen their border defenses for permanence and stability and have the right to permanently monitor the armaments of neighboring countries internationally.

No Use of Force Abroad (2) No country's force should exceed its own borders; otherwise, it will be considered an aggressor. Conclusion of Disarmament Agreements (3) Formal agreements must be concluded to eliminate aggression and offensive weapons.

National Tendency Towards Peace Roosevelt said that after recent events, we are moving further away from the ultimate goals of ourselves and former President Wilson. Roosevelt said, "Those with shallow views will say that the failure of disarmament is due to the development of nationalism. Believing this, it is necessary that the people everywhere agree with nationalism. However, judging from the current national trends in various countries, this is not entirely the case. The danger to peace lies not in the people but in certain political leaders."

Special Class of People Revered Roosevelt continued, "Among the 1.5 billion people in the world, I dare to say that at least 90% are satisfied with the current territories, and if other countries reduce armaments, these nations would be happy to reduce their forces. The danger to world peace arises from the psychology of fear or the remaining 10% of the people may not be in disagreement. The worry is that their leaders want to invade other countries' lands to expand their own territories. These leaders use various reasons to oppose disarmament, even hindering other nations who have agreed to disarmament and non-aggression principles. If nine-tenths of the world's people can make the remaining one-tenth advocate their own ideas without being manipulated by their leaders, then a permanent and effective peace can be established worldwide." (Agence Havas, 29th)

Satisfaction in Geneva

(Geneva) People here are very satisfied with the speech delivered yesterday by U.S. President Roosevelt, particularly emphasizing the following words: "The League of Nations encourages countries to sign non-aggression treaties and form disarmament agreements, which can be regarded as the cornerstone of world peace. The United States is not a member of the League of Nations and has no intention of joining, but in the event of non-purely political issues and other issues that clearly represent the views and interests of all nations in the world rather than the special class purposes of certain political leaders and not the purposes of imperialism, the United States is willing to cooperate with the League of Nations." (Agence Havas, 29th)

A Glimpse of Various Newspaper Opinions

(Paris) French newspapers all have minor criticisms of the speech delivered by President Roosevelt on the birthday of former President Wilson. "Le Temps" expressed sympathy for the declining ability of the League of Nations but criticized the United States for refusing to join international organizations with strength, saying that the failure of the disarmament conference was mostly due to the inactivity of the United States. The United States' refusal to ratify the Treaty of Versailles or form a strong Anglo-American front to resist Germany's aggression is an obstacle to the world peace organization. "Le Matin," while expressing satisfaction with President Roosevelt's remarks, concluded that the United States should not ignore France's past experiences and dare not readily accept its words. France will judge the foreign policy of the United States based on its actual actions rather than its pleasant words. (National Telegraph, 29th)

All newspapers in Rome and Italy welcomed President Roosevelt's speech. "Il Giornale d'Italia" said that the main points in his speech completely coincided with the views of Italian leader Mussolini, especially on the two issues of revising treaties and disarmament. (National Telegraph, 29th)

(Washington) After President Roosevelt delivered his speech yesterday at the Board of Directors of the "Wilson Foundation," the initial response in the United States was extremely favorable. Only "World Telegram" expressed slight dissatisfaction, saying that the President's speech "failed to make a clearer reference to the gathering war clouds in Europe and the Far East, which contain serious dangers, which is a pity." Fortunately, the Monroe Doctrine, sometimes used by the United States as a unilateral tool to send troops to the republics of the New World, was not explicitly criticized in Roosevelt's speech, but such an interpretation of the Monroe Doctrine has been written off. The newspaper also said that the United States can remain untainted with Latin America, and then it can have the latitude to speak righteously against the imperialism of Britain, France, Italy, the German arrogance of Hitler, and those who profit from war. (Agence Havas, 29th)

The Achievements of the League of Nations Are Thus

(Geneva) The Secretariat of the League of Nations has recently compiled and published a booklet on the various activities of the League of Nations this year. According to the report, 1933 was the most burdensome and criticized period for the League of Nations since its establishment. During this year, there were two important international conferences: (1) the Disarmament Conference and (2) the World Economic and Monetary Conference. There were also three important political disputes: (1) the Sino-Japanese conflict in the Far East, (2) the dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia over the Gran Chaco, and (3) the dispute between Peru and Colombia over the Leticia port. The Disarmament Conference made significant progress on the system for monitoring armaments, but it encountered serious difficulties after Germany withdrew. As for the World Economic and Monetary Conference, it adjourned without achieving its main objectives but made considerable achievements on the wheat and silver issues. In addition, there are other achievements, namely (1) the convention on limiting the manufacture of narcotics and suppressing their sale, which was concluded in 1931, has been implemented and has come into effect, and (2) the League of Nations Covenant has been ratified by Argentina, and the country has rejoined the League. This is the tangible result of the League of Nations this year. (Agence Havas, 29th)

Paraguay and Bolivia Extend Truce

Bolivia has formally accepted, while the Paraguayan government only allows an extension of eight days. (Agence Havas, 29th)

The Origin of the Crown Prince's Title

According to the Japanese-language Shanghai Daily yesterday, the Crown Prince held his naming ceremony on the 29th, named Akihito, and titled Tsugu-no-miya. According to a conversation with Tomi-no-miya in the Imperial Household Agency, the origin of the title of the Crown Prince is based on the edict issued on January 3, Meiji 3, and based on the I Ching. The title Tsugu-no-miya is based on Han Yu's "Pacification of Huaixi Stele" ["Holy Son, Sacred, Inheriting Successively"]. Also, the Doctrine of the Mean has ["Good in continuing his will,"], and the History of the Han Dynasty has ["Emperor who Inherited the Body"], so Tsugu-no-miya is the title of the Crown Prince.

Liu Guitang's Troops Flee from Chicheng to Yangyuan

Japanese Troops Increase in Eastern Chahar

Zhang Renjie's Troops Fill Defense in Chicheng

Liu's Mother Instructs Her Son Not to Defect

Peiping Correspondence: The Japanese troops who invaded Eastern Chahar have shown no preparation to withdraw. Recently, they have established a bandit suppression headquarters in the Heihe area, indicating a desire to occupy it for a long time. Although some of the puppet troops in the 24th district of Guyuan have withdrawn to Dolon, the Japanese troops in the Xifengkou area have slightly increased. After Liu Guitang's troops left Chicheng, the Chahar provincial authorities have transferred the troops of Zhang Yunrong and Zhang Renjie to advance, and Zhang Yunrong's troops have entered Chicheng to maintain order and handle the aftermath.

Liu Guitang, nicknamed "Black Seven," is from Caozhou, Shantung. He is 53 years old and extremely fierce. He was originally a major bandit in Western Shantung, repeatedly surrendering and rebelling. To date, he has rebelled more than fifty-one times. Last year, he fled from Shantung and entered Jehol. After Jehol fell, Liu falsely surrendered to the rebel army and defrauded the Japanese army of a large number of weapons and ammunition. This spring, he entered Dolon from Jehol. When Feng Yuxiang organized the Anti-Japanese Allied Army in Zhangjiakou, Liu telegraphed to support the righteous cause. When Song Zheyuan returned to Chahar, Liu's troops were reorganized accordingly and stationed in Chicheng. Song repeatedly telegraphed, inviting him to Zhangjiakou for a meeting, but Liu never responded. This time, when the Japanese and puppet troops invaded Eastern Chahar, the Chahar provincial authorities, in order to consolidate the defenses of Eastern Chahar, dispatched Zhang Yunrong and Zhang Renjie's troops to reinforce the defenses. On the other hand, due to Liu's unclear attitude, they ordered him to move to Yangyuan in Western Chahar. They telegraphed Liu repeatedly, but Liu did not reply. Liu suspected that the Chahar provincial authorities had ulterior motives and was quite uneasy. He convened a meeting of his subordinates, intending to flee eastward and join the puppet rebels. At that time, Liu's mother was still in the army. Upon hearing the news, she strongly disagreed and instructed her son, saying that although she was over seventy years old, she would rather be a bandit in China than a traitor. Although Liu was crude, he was filial to his mother, so he stopped the plan to flee eastward and sent his mother to Tianjin. On the 25th, he led his troops to leave Chicheng and fled southwestward. Liu's troops totaled eight to nine thousand people. At the time of the rebellion, Xia Ziming's brigade, which was stationed in Longsuo, did not defect and remained in its original defense, expressing obedience to the orders of the Chahar provincial authorities. Zhang Junjie and Liu's representative, Tian Gangyi, were also in Xia's place. Liu only led five to six thousand people to flee westward, first to Yangtianbao, south of Chicheng, attempting to flee into the war zone for cover. Yesterday (27th), they fled to the Dishuiya and Hongshaling areas and were besieged by local militias and Japanese puppet troops, splitting into two groups. One group fled back to Yangtianbao, and the other group fled towards Qingkou. Today (28th), Liu himself has led his troops to Yongningzhen, west of the railway, with only two to three thousand remaining troops, in a very miserable state, and there is a tendency to flee in separate directions to the Yangyuan area. After receiving the alert of Liu's troops' rebellion, the Chahar provincial authorities, in addition to ordering Zhang Yunrong and Zhang Renjie's troops to quickly enter Chicheng to maintain order, also ordered the troops of Feng Zhan

The Ministry of Communications Orders the China Merchants Bureau to Stop Hiring Foreign Seamen

Foreign seamen whose contracts have expired should not be rehired.

Vacancies should be filled by promoting Chinese staff.

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the Ministry of Communications, in order to safeguard the shipping industry, has recently issued an order to the China Merchants Bureau to stop hiring foreign captains and seamen, and that when the contracts of current captains and seamen expire, they should not be renewed. Instead, Chinese seamen should be promoted according to their qualifications. The original text is recorded as follows: “According to the China Merchant Ship Drivers Association, at the beginning of the China Merchants Bureau's establishment, most of the crew members of all levels were foreigners. This was because the Chinese people lacked nautical talent and had no choice but to borrow talent from other countries, resulting in the loss of sovereignty, which is deeply regrettable. Fortunately, in recent years, the Chinese people have worked hard and diligently, and more and more people have acquired nautical knowledge. Chinese people began to serve as crew members of all levels in the bureau. Afterwards, after being managed by the national government, the principle was to have Chinese people serve as crew members of all levels, and vacancies were mainly filled by promotion according to qualifications. As a result, more and more Chinese people served as crew members of the bureau, and many Chinese people were also promoted to captains. We are fortunate that nautical sovereignty is gradually being recovered, which is a glory for the country. Since Chinese people have served as captains, they have been prudent and careful, and their performance has been excellent. In the past, when foreigners served as captains, accidents occurred frequently, such as the sinking of the Xinhua, Xinji, Xinchang, and Xinkang ships, which is clear evidence. Furthermore, according to the laws of various countries, in consideration of sovereignty, the principle is to have their own citizens serve as captains. As for the high salaries paid to foreign captains, it is a minor matter to waste the national treasury. It is now heard that the bureau has the motive of employing foreign captains again, such as recently hiring a foreign captain for the Xinfeng ship. This not only violates the original system, but also fears that nautical sovereignty will be lost again. We are deeply saddened by this. We do not know what Liu, the general manager of the bureau, is thinking, disregarding the country's nautical rights? The association has witnessed this situation and finds it difficult to remain silent. We hereby submit this report to the Ministry, ordering the general manager that foreign captains in office should not be rehired after their contracts expire, and that when there are captain vacancies, Chinese crew members should be promoted according to their qualifications and no foreigners should be hired again, so as to safeguard nautical rights. This would be a great blessing for the country." Therefore, in addition to the approval, this order is hereby issued to the bureau to investigate and submit its opinions for approval. This is the order.

Yongkang and Hongyuan Ships Rescue Hongli

Hengshan Ship Collision Case

Dingsheng Claims 50,000

The grounding of the Sanbei Company's Hongli ship in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has been reported in this newspaper. Now, according to telegrams, due to the rapid and shallow Yongji Shoal, rescue is difficult. Therefore, the Yongkang ship has been dispatched to assist. A more detailed description is as follows:

Grounded at Xiache Bay

The grounding of the Hongli ship occurred in the Yangtze River, in the waters of Xiache Bay near Jianli. Due to the sharp drop in the river level, the ship was grounded. Initially, the Shashi Sanbei Branch planned to send the Hongheng ship to tow it, but because the Hongheng ship was larger and the water was very shallow there, the Hongyuan ship was ordered to sail to tow it. However, due to the rapid current and shallow water, it could not be rescued. The owner of the Hongyuan ship telegraphed the Shashi Branch to report.

Send Barges to Unload Cargo

After receiving the telegram from Hongyuan, the Shashi Branch dispatched a batch of laborers and released the No. 8 towing barge to Xiache Bay, ordering the workers to first unload all the cargo inside the Hongli ship, and then tow it, so that the ship's hull would be lighter and easier to tow. However, the barge could not get close, so they telegraphed Shashi again, requesting the dispatch of the shallow-water small ship Yongkang to tow it quickly. The Shanghai Bureau has already telegraphed the Hankou Branch to do so.

Hengshan Collision Claims

The company's Hengshan ship sank the Dingsheng ship in Zhenjiang. Now the shipowner has sent a formal letter of claim to Shanghai, stating that the Dingsheng sank, with a loss of more than 30,000 yuan in ship hull damage, and a loss of more than 10,000 yuan in lost passengers, cargo, crew luggage, and clothing, for a total of more than 50,000 yuan. They are demanding compensation from Sanbei.

Two Railways Reduce Freight Rates for Cotton Yarn and Stone Pencils

Promoting Education and Encouraging Domestic Products

Eight Percent Discount on Piece Goods and Cotton Yarn

Effective January 1st of Next Year

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, in order to reduce the freight rates for domestic stone pencils and piece goods and cotton yarn, has decided to implement this starting on January 1st of next year. Yesterday, it specially notified the Traffic Department to comply with the following original text:

Domestic Stone Pencils: It has been found that pencils were originally listed as Second Class (boxed) and Third Class (ordinary) for freight charges. Now, the Ministry of Railways, considering that the stone pencils produced near Changxindian are domestic products and daily necessities for primary schools, has ordered all railways to allow them to be listed as special prices in accordance with the special price method for educational instruments, books, and printed matter formulated by the former Ministry of Communications. The freight rate is set at 2.7 hao per 100 kilograms per kilometer, to be implemented on a trial basis for one year, in order to show the intention of promoting education and encouraging domestic products. The bureau has received the order and now sets the implementation date as January 1st, 1934.

Piece Goods and Cotton Yarn: With regard to the transportation of piece goods and cotton yarn on the Beijing-Shanghai Line, those who report for transportation with a certificate from the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Association will be charged at a special price with an additional 20% discount. This was previously approved by the ministry. Now, the merchants believe that the freight rates for these items on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line are different from those on the Beijing-Shanghai Line and request equal treatment. After careful assessment by the bureau, it is believed that there is no need to reduce the freight rates for cotton yarn and the special price for piece goods and cotton yarn on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line. However, the 20% discount based on the certificate from the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Association can be applied to ensure fairness. This has been approved by the Ministry of Railways and will be calculated at an 8% discount to promote the industry. This will also be implemented from New Year's Day next year.

National Private Electricity Industry Federation

Establishment of the Economic Committee

Cooperation with the Financial Community to Utilize Capital

Lu Bohong, Liu Chongyou, etc. are Committee Members

The circumstances of the fifth annual meeting of the National Private Electricity Industry Federation held in Hankou this year have been reported in various newspapers. Representatives from Various Sectors

Representatives attending the meeting included Liu Chongyou from Beiping Huajian Electric Company, Wang Shucheng from Hankou Jiji Water and Electricity Company, Lu Bohong from Shanghai Chinese Electric Company, Weng Yousan from Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, Tong Shoumin from Pudong Electric Company, Liu Chonglun from Fuzhou Electric Company, Ju Xinfu from Ningbo Yongyao Power Company, Li Yanshi from Wuwei Electric Company, Shen Sifang, Director-General of the Electric Federation, and Li Wenzhi from the Shanghai Communications Office. Wang Shucheng was elected as the temporary chairman, and Li Wenzhi was the recorder.

Tasks of the Economic Committee

The chairman reported briefly that since the establishment of the Federation, more than five years have passed, and various committees, such as the Technology and Hygiene Committee, the Education Committee, and the Statistics Committee, have been established one after another. The purpose of the Economic Committee is to seek the sound development of the economic organization of the national electricity industry. Its tasks are: (1) guiding matters related to the research of electricity industry economic organization, (2) assisting and coordinating matters related to the economy of the same industry, (3) communicating and cooperating matters between the electricity industry and the financial community, (4) preparing for the organization of the electricity industry bank, (5) planning and promoting the electrification of rural areas. In general, it aims to improve the organization within the same industry and to liaise with the banking community to utilize the idle funds concentrated in urban areas to invest in the most promising and stable electricity production business. Then,

Election of Officers

Japanese Poisonous Plan to Annihilate Volunteers

Cigarettes are Not Allowed to Reduce Taxes

Ministry of Finance Replies to Chamber of Commerce Telegram

The Ministry of Finance telegraphed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce in reply, saying, "Cigarettes are luxury consumer goods, and all countries levy heavy taxes on them. The taxes levied in our country are still light. At present, due to the urgent need for funds for bandit suppression and construction, the first-level tax has been increased to 160 yuan and the second-level tax to 80 yuan. The Central Political Conference has resolved to follow this plan. It is inappropriate to approve the request to postpone the implementation or reduce the tax. In this tax increase case, four measures have been stipulated for investigating and cracking down on tax evasion and smuggled cigarettes: (1) Setting up cigarette factories is limited to four places: Shanghai, Tianjin, Qingdao, and Hankou. No cigarette factories are allowed to be set up in other places, and existing ones should be ordered to relocate within a time limit, and if they fail to do so, the government will recover them at an appraised price. (2) The capital of newly established cigarette factories must be more than 500,000. (3) Handmade cigarettes should be strictly restricted and no further registration should be allowed, or they should be banned immediately. (4) Tax police should strictly investigate and ban counterfeit and tax-evading handmade cigarettes. Tax evasion investigation teams should be set up in places where there are no tax police. The above items have been ordered by the Ministry to be carried out in sequence. According to the report from Yu Tingsheng, chairman of the Cigarette Industry Association, the association has resolved to comply with the newly increased tax rates. Special reply."

Cement Merchants Request Exemption from Increased Unified Tax

Tax Administration's Approval Rejected Yesterday

Matters Concerned Should Not Be Made to Revoke the Order

Bank Guarantee Still Allowed for Bookkeeping

The China Cement Manufacturers Association received a reply from the Tax Administration yesterday, saying, "I have read the report. The increase in cement tax was originally a last resort for the government. At a time when the national treasury is strained, the construction of major projects, and military operations to suppress bandits all require funds, manufacturers should make an effort to help. Moreover, the newly revised cement unified tax rate is the same throughout the country, and all factories bear the same burden. Manufacturers only have the intention of collecting and paying taxes on behalf of consumers, and the actual tax burden is borne by consumers, so manufacturers should not feel too much pain. Moreover, this administration has a bookkeeping method for manufacturers to pay the unified tax. If manufacturers can find a bank guarantee, they can be allowed to keep accounts, so they will not suffer the difficulty of paying the unified tax in advance. Matters related to general cases, the request to revoke the order is difficult to forward. It is hoped that manufacturers will be properly persuaded to work hard to comply. This is what is expected."

Rectifying Court Opening Times and Order

The Shanghai Lawyers Association has written to the President of the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court regarding the delay in court opening times and the occupation of lawyers' seats by police officers, requesting that the President correct this. The original letter and instruction are recorded below. (1) The Lawyers Association's official letter is regarding the fact that criminal cases do not open on time and police officers occupy lawyers' seats, requesting correction. According to a proposal by member Gao Junxiang, criminal cases in the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court often do not open in accordance with the scheduled time after the scheduled opening time. Defense lawyers sit idly in court due to the delay in opening. If there is another case in another court or in another division of the same court before or after the scheduled time, they will be hindered from performing their duties. Furthermore, it is feared that there will be no shortage of plaintiffs and defendants who lose their jobs due to the delay in the lawsuit. Furthermore, the lawyers' seats in the criminal court are specially for lawyers appearing in court to perform their duties and should not be occupied by anyone. However, recently, these lawyers' seats have often been occupied by police officers, in order to maintain order and the execution of lawyers' duties. It is proposed that the court correct these matters. After deliberation by the Joint Meeting of the First 156th Executive Committee of the Association, it was resolved that the matter should be forwarded to the court for review and correction. This is for the convenience of the public. (2) Instruction from the Second Special District Court, Instruction No. 149 from the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court, to the Shanghai Lawyers Association, regarding a letter requesting correction of court opening times and occupation of lawyers' seats. I have read the letter. The requested matters have been separately ordered to be handled. This is the order for your information.

New Information on Economic and Credit Cooperatives

Striving for Practicality and Not Just Empty Talk

Striving to Facilitate Members

Since its opening, the China Economic and Credit Cooperative has had hundreds of members. The cooperative is quite capable of fulfilling its mutual assistance responsibilities in the face of members' difficulties. Members who are unemployed can request job referrals. The method is for members to fill out a job referral application form. Except for those who lack ability or have excessive expectations, the cooperative will help them find employment. When they find employment, they can entrust the cooperative to sign the contract. After finding employment, no remuneration is required. However, requests for referrals cannot be answered within a limited time, nor can the job introduced by the cooperative be transferred to others. The cooperative has eight types of cooperative loans. At present, only credit loans and bill discounts are available. Recently, many members have requested loans. Except for those who have no ability to repay, the cooperative does not reject them. However, the amount of the loan is fixed according to regulations, so it is insufficient to allocate, so the amount of loan requested by each person must be slightly reduced so that all members can benefit.

The cooperative has legal and medical consultants to provide free consultation to members. If they are still unclear after consultation, they can ask again. It is said that Xu Xueping has been hired as an accounting consultant, and Zhang Zhirang, Ma Junshuo, Li Caixia, Zhang Diming, Qian Baohe, Sun Zuji, Yin Shijie, and Qiu Hanping, etc. as legal consultants, and Yang Baoheng, Chen Siming, and Song Hongfu, etc. as medical consultants. There are also commercial and study abroad consultants who are being hired.

It is also heard that the cooperative plans to hold an economic cooperation movement week because some people from all walks of life do not fully understand economic cooperation. It plans to publish a special issue and hold lectures. People from all walks of life, such as Kong Xiangxi, Wu Tiecheng, Chu Minyi, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, and Pan Gongzhan, etc., have expressed their sympathy and participated in the sponsorship.

In addition, for those who believe in cooperativeism but are unable to pay the membership savings, they are also given the opportunity to enjoy mutual assistance. Therefore, an amateur inspirational association is attached. Those who join the association are like joining ordinary social organizations, without having to save monthly, and the rights they enjoy are almost the same as those of members, except for life insurance and maturity interest. More than 100 people have joined. At present, in order to promote cooperation, it is planned to solicit members. The association has supplementary schools, current affairs lectures, Sunday entertainment, mutual assistance fund rules, and bonus rules, etc. It is also heard that Ye Yunfeng, Zheng Tianren, Qiu Huasheng, and Wu Yuwen, etc. have been hired from among the members as the association's secretaries, and Xiao Yihan, Qiu Jinxian, and Zhuang Zutong, etc. as reviewers.

Jincheng Grand Theater to Open Soon

Architecture and Equipment Exceed Expectations

The Jincheng Grand Theater at the intersection of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road was founded with exclusive Chinese capital. The construction has been going on for half a year, and the entire project has been 90% completed. The grandeur of the architecture, the richness of the decoration, and the novelty of the equipment can be called unique. The entire building is three-dimensional and towers into the clouds. There are four huge pillars on the facade, which are magnificent and magnificent, adding to the heroic posture. At night, the light shines thousands of feet, reflecting the Chinese and English characters of the golden neon lights, adding to the beauty. The escalators in the hall are also decorated with neon lights, which shine inside and outside, making it a magnificent sight. The arrangement of the electric lights in the theater is extremely exquisite and delicate, with concealed lighting that is elegant and pleasant. The corridors throughout the theater are decorated with high-quality carpets, which are light, soft, and unparalleled. There are more than 1,800 seats, all with spring cushions and brightly colored seat covers, which are comfortable and luxurious, unprecedented. The style, size, and arrangement of the seats are particularly carefully considered, so as to achieve the goal of no seat being bad. The sound equipment used is a German solid-state giant machine, which has a sturdy sound, lasts for a long time, and produces a clear sound that is neither sharp nor turbid. Even the slightest breath can be heard easily. As for all the noisy echoes, they are all covered by the non-flammable sound-absorbing paper on the walls, and the countless small holes on the screen are sufficient to assist in the perfection of the sound. The projector used by the theater is the German Anaman No. 5, which has long been popular all over the world, but the No. 5 is the latest product released in March last year, which is much more advanced than previous products. The light is also strong, and the objects projected on the screen are all three-dimensional, with clear distances and clear characters. The theater not only planned carefully for sound, light, and seats, but also paid special attention to hygiene management and fire protection equipment, so that the audience can get rid of all worries and feel comfortable both physically and mentally. The heating and cooling equipment is the latest type, and the cooling can be increased or decreased freely, and the temperature can be raised or lowered appropriately according to the climate outside the theater and the standards of hygiene. Being in it is like enjoying the pleasure of a gentle breeze and without the pain of dryness and annoyance, which is especially suitable for the physique of Chinese people. In the future, when it is put into use, everyone will be satisfied. The so-called heating is not the ordinary hot water radiator, but a special equipment that transports hot air into the theater. There is an automatic device that can freely control the hot air and the temperature is moderate, warm and spring-like. Now, the theater will open as soon as the internal layout is completed. It is said that the first major contribution of the opening will be the Lianhua special giant film [Return].

The association's chairman Kong Xiangxi, fundraising committee chairman Fei Meide, committee members Wu Tiecheng's wife, Zhao Jinqing, Lin Kanghou, Bei Zuyi, Cao Yunxiang, Luo Yunyan, Du Yuesheng, Chen Liting, Pastor, Zhang Xuelou's wife, Guo Shun's wife, Zhu Ziliang, Fei Wusheng's wife, Miss Smith, Yan En's wife, Chen Bingzhang's wife, Mrs. Lowry, Mrs. Xu Jianping, Mrs. Edward, Miss Kerr, Mrs. and Mrs. Raynal, Mr. Zhang Jia'ao, Mrs. Song Ziwen, Miss Tang Luoguan, Mrs. Song Hu, Mrs. Studebaker, etc., as well as secretaries Xu Jianping, Chen Tiesheng, Wang Guanyi, Zhao Jian, Chen Zhengfan, Zhang Yueru, Han Chao, Ding Bingnan, Liu Jinfang, and Wang Aitian, etc., all carry out their work in separate groups, and are very busy in order to achieve their goals and meet the needs. In recent times, the country has been plagued by many misfortunes, the status of children has declined, and there is no way to revive the nation. If this continues, what will become of the country? Therefore, five years ago, I gathered comrades to establish this association, using my personal abilities to assist the government, which has no time to do so. The benefits will not only bless the children of the whole country, but also rebuild the Republic of China. I respectfully request this."

Fundraising Notice

The foundation of a country lies first in supporting the nation, promoting civil rights, and solving people's livelihood. The basis of the nation is children, the evolution of civil rights is in children, and the implementation of people's livelihood depends on children. Therefore, to support the nation, we must first love children; to promote civil rights, we must first protect children; to solve people's livelihood, we must first educate children. Love, protection, and education are all rights that children should enjoy, and they are also the missions that the association has undertaken since its establishment. It is found that in the past, all provinces also had infant halls, orphanages, Mengxue elementary schools, kindergartens, etc. for children, which also had the intention of protection and education. However, due to changes in national affairs, the main reason was that they were not here, so old habits, such as the rich accumulating slaves and abusing maids, and the poor drowning children and selling daughters, and unscrupulous people taking the opportunity to make a profit, still persisted. Alas, who has no parents, who is not a child, and to blame, the room is here. This association was established in 1928. Up to now, it has been five years, with division of labor and cooperation, and each is responsible for its own duties. Special protection, inspection and relief, and recently, we have revised children's laws and established juvenile courts to continue to protect them. We have established child welfare education and care homes, and child welfare health and medical clinics, and hired experts to compile children's books and other children's stories and children's songs. We have also established a child welfare park in Yangzuo, specializing in taking in the young children of female workers, and providing them with education and care. We have also proposed that April 4 be designated as [Children's Day] and publish the Modern Parents Monthly

A Review of the Past Year

— Shu

January 1, 1933. The sound of cannons destroying world peace originated from a corner of the Far East, beyond Shanhaiguan. This cannonball was similar to the one fired at Sarajevo, and the seriousness of the situation was extremely similar. The world's powers mostly focused their attention on the changes in the Far Eastern political situation. However, the revelation of facts seemed to exceed general expectations. That is, after the Shanhaiguan incident occurred, the explosive power of this cannonball only reached the east bank of the Luan River. And the powers that focused their attention on the East, only focused their attention. There was no further indication. Until the Rehe problem followed the sound of the Shanhaiguan cannons. When the sound of cannons in Rehe was booming, it was the time when the Geneva Disarmament Conference was being held. We don't need to study the technical issues of this disarmament, but it is a unique and extraordinary thing in the world to talk about morality while the flames of war are raging on one side. It is enough to prove the bleak future of disarmament. We certainly know that disputes between countries can only be resolved by force. However, in this disheveled and struggling state, what is somewhat comforting is that world justice has not been completely buried. That is, the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly on February 24, with a unanimous vote of forty-two, declared the so-called [Manchukuo] to be a forgery and confirmed the report and recommendations made by the Nineteen-Member Committee. Although there is no actual binding force, it can still represent the general public opinion of the world. Since then, the world situation has deteriorated, and the crisis of economic panic has gradually been exposed. The United States of America, possessing almost half of the world's gold, experienced an unprecedented financial turmoil at the beginning of the new President Roosevelt's inauguration. Even millionaires became destitute overnight. What is the impact of such an event on the world? It is almost inevitable that the United States will abandon the gold standard and adopt an inflationary policy.

Since the world economy has been greatly shocked by the US financial panic, what will the future hold? Even the people involved are mostly apprehensive. Advanced countries are even more concerned. Therefore, they regard the World Economic Conference as the key to solving current difficult problems. If the countries can truly abandon their past prejudices and implement international cooperation, then production agreements can be established, sales markets may be equalized, and technical issues such as currency exchange rates will not be difficult to find appropriate solutions. The current economic difficulties may not be insurmountable. Unfortunately, the historical disputes between countries are too deep, and the conflicts of interest are too fierce. As a result, international cooperation has only become a diplomatic formality, and economic nationalism has become the foundation of economic alliances. The war debt problem cannot be solved at the Economic Conference, and inflation and stabilizing international exchange rates have become mutually opposed. Coupled with the difficulty of reducing tariff barriers, the cracks between countries have become even deeper as a result.

At this time, the United States could only try its best to calm its already exposed panic. Britain was engaged in consolidating its economic alliance within the empire. France wanted to take the lead in European finance. Germany was eager for an economic way out. Japan continued its military adventure policy. The Soviet Union also shifted from cold observation to focusing on war preparations. The Eastern issue seemed to be a hidden current on the surface, but in reality, it was deteriorating. Although the twenty-second year of the Republic of China has barely passed, based on the past experience and lessons of hardship, we can predict the future. Under this four-sided pressure, how will our country strive to eliminate the current crisis in the coming year?

Shanxi Coal Industry Representatives Petition for Reduction of Shanxi Coal Freight

(Nanjing) Yang Renxian and other representatives of the coal industry from Jinyangquan Station in Shanxi came to Nanjing to petition, requesting a reduction in Shanxi coal freight. According to reporters, the amount of coal stored in Shanxi accounts for more than 58% of the country. The province's Zuoyun and other 57 counties are all coal-producing areas. There are a total of 1,523 mining companies or kiln factories, with a total of 37,518 workers. The annual output is 3,745,475 tons. The sluggish sales of domestic coal are actually due to the low-priced dumping of foreign coal, which is difficult for domestic coal to resist. Rural bankruptcy is also affected. Excessive freight rates prevent long-distance sales, and excessive taxes increase costs, making sales difficult. (Central News Agency dispatch, 30th)

The Naval Department Will Send Personnel to Italy to Study

(Nanjing) China and Italy have friendly relations. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, in order to enhance the friendly relations between the two countries, instructed the new Italian ambassador to China to express goodwill to the naval authorities and welcome the Chinese Navy to send personnel to study in the Italian Navy and will give special preferential treatment. This is the first time that the Chinese Navy has sent personnel to study in Italy. The Naval Department is currently selecting outstanding personnel and preparing their luggage. They can set off in January or February of the new year. In the future, the friendly relations between China and Italy will naturally increase. (Central News Agency dispatch, 30th)

Dutch Ambassador Du Peyke Arrives in Beijing

(Nanjing) The Dutch Ambassador to China, Du Peyke, arrived in Beijing from Ping on the 29th and stayed at the Huilong Hotel in Xiaguan. He paid a visit to Wang on the morning of the 30th, and Wang gave him a welcoming reception. Chen Gongbo, Zhu Jiahua, Wang Shijie, Xu Mo, Liu Shishun, Zhang Pingqun, Lin Jiongshi and other seven people accompanied him. Du then took a fast train to Shanghai at Shenshi. (Special dispatch, 30th)

The Xiangbao-Hong Road in Hunan is Under Construction

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways has formulated three methods for carrying out the construction of the Xiangbao-Hong Road in Hunan Province: (1) All technical and road planning shall be reviewed and approved by the Ministry of Railways in accordance with the central government's resolution. (2) The Ministry of Railways shall supervise the construction. (3) All implementation work shall be entrusted to the Hunan Construction Department to be responsible for carrying out, and the Hunan Provincial Government shall be instructed to follow the instructions of the Construction Department. (Central News Agency dispatch, 30th)

Litvinov Sternly Denounces Japan's Breach of Faith and Provocation Against Russia

Using Cunning Means to Seize the Chinese Eastern Railway

Japanese Policy is a Shadow in International Politics

(Moscow) Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov reported on the international situation to the Central Executive Committee today, directly denouncing Japan's breach of faith, saying that Japan had promised not to harm the interests of Russians in Manchuria. The Soviet Union deeply believed in its words. Unexpectedly, after the September 18th Incident, Japan directly attacked the interests of the Soviet Union and hindered the business of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Japan wanted to obtain the Chinese Eastern Railway as a gift from the Soviet Union. Therefore, it did not hesitate to use cunning means to seize the railway with the help of police, bandits and the Manchurian Self-Defense Army. Russian-Japanese relations are now attracting worldwide attention because Japan's policy is the darkest shadow in the international political sky. Litvinov spoke in a satisfactory tone about the restoration of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, but unfortunately, China is still suffering from the invasion of neighboring enemies and the internal disputes are serious. Litvinov also said that Japan has heavily concentrated its forces near the Manchurian border, which endangers the Soviet border. The Soviet Union has to send a large delegation to consolidate its border defense. The Soviet Union does not threaten Japan, but Japan's first step must be to show its will for peace in fact. Japan must stop its violent police activities on the Chinese Eastern Railway, restore the infringed Soviet Russian rights, reopen negotiations on the fair sale and purchase of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and sign the non-aggression treaty proposed by the Soviet Union two years ago. Today, we have an impression that the Japanese authorities in Manchuria clearly want to incite behavior that is more serious than protest. The Soviet Union is currently only adopting a defensive plan, while Japan is preparing for an aggressive war. Litvinov then compared Germany and Japan and issued a warning to the Socialist Party, saying that if the National Socialist Party wants to realize its dream of colonizing Ukraine or elsewhere, the Soviet Russian government will definitely oppose it. Litvinov finally mentioned Geneva, saying that the disarmament conference may be revived temporarily, but even if it can be revived, it will only be a conference to reorganize armaments rather than reduce armaments. Only when all countries no longer regard the non-aggression treaty as waste paper can there be a real discussion of the disarmament issue. Under such circumstances, the Soviet Russian government has to increase and improve its necessary national defense, because the Soviet Union cannot guarantee that there will not be a time when it must maintain Stalin's declaration that the Soviet Union will not give up an inch of land. (Reuters)

Full Text of Russian Foreign Minister's Speech

(Moscow) Today, Foreign People's Commissar Litvinov reported on the international situation and Soviet foreign policy at the General Assembly of the Central Executive Committee. Litvinov elaborated on the current stage of the development of international life and said that the era of bourgeois pacifism has passed. The central issues of diplomatic negotiations and conferences in Geneva are no longer disarmament, but expansion and reorganization of armaments. At the same time, newly rising political parties, new factions, and new figures have risen with a new military spirit and new ideologies. These newly rising political parties declared anti-communist movements, but under the cover of such struggles, they secretly carried out narrowly scoped nationalist aspirations, namely revising treaties and seizing territories. And its revision also includes those that are explicitly stipulated in the treaty, or even those that are not recorded. Litvinov continued, [If the fortune of war once smiles on them, then they will not be limited to the territories held by the Marxists they hate, and will also involve the territories of the bourgeoisie, even the territories ruled by rulers with similar ideas are inevitable. This is the situation in a certain European country. At the same time, there is a country that does not borrow any psychological or even theoretical complex preparation work, and from the beginning takes the revision of the border, the replacement of the agreement, and its implementation, without diplomats but only relying on generals. These generals always lead their troops across the vast Asian continent, regarding all borders and the interests of the people as worn-out shoes,] (omitted) Litvinov continued, [The key to Soviet foreign policy has been fully expressed by Stalin's concise formula, namely, we do not want foreign territory, but we also do not want to lose an inch of our territory, so we never hope for war. As for our territory, we have been able to guarantee it with increasing military power, and can make foreign forces dare not approach and covet it. This kind of military power can also teach our neighbors near and far, and they can live in their own borders in peace for decades. We are working hard to establish and maintain friendship with all countries, so we focus on consolidating diplomatic relations with countries in the world that truly want to maintain peace and at the same time prepare to oppose those who destroy peace, and practice the highest degree of amity. In the past and present, we have never refused organized international cooperation to defend peace, and we have never refused to use these existing or formable international associations and organizations, if we have reason to deeply believe that these combinations are beneficial to peace,

Amity with the United States, Turkey, France, and Italy Litvinov mentioned the relationship between the Soviet Union and various countries, starting with the United States. He said that the United States intends to maintain peace and believes that its good relations with the Soviet Union can be a powerful factor in maintaining peace, so it attaches great importance to the cooperation between the United States and the Soviet Union in this regard. As for our side, we also take maintaining peace as the starting point for attaching importance to this matter, and believe that the restoration of diplomatic relations between the United States and the Soviet Union is of value. When Litvinov mentioned Turkey, he said, [We believe that the Soviet-Turkish diplomatic relations are a model for our diplomatic relations with other countries. The policy of friendship and mutual trust can also build a foundation for effective cooperation in international politics. If one party proposes a proposal to consolidate peace, it can obtain the assistance of the other party in advance. If such relations can be established among the people of all countries, the problem of peace will be solved.] Litvinov continued, [When we describe the gradual and important increase in relations with other countries, we should first discuss France. This year, our relationship with France has made great and rapid progress. The alliance between the Soviet Union and France is maintained by a common desire to sincerely seek peace. We do not need to worry that the repeated changes in the French government will affect the smooth development of this close relationship. Recently, Herriot and Cot's visit to the Soviet Union has given new impetus to the friendship between France and the Soviet Union. It is expected that the progress of this friendship will be even more rapid, because the elements that threaten peace are now gathering. Our diplomatic relations with Italy have been unusually stable for ten years. Whether in economic or political issues, there has never been a change or tension. When I recently visited Italy, I received a warm welcome. This is enough to prove that both countries are willing to develop their relations in economic and political aspects.

British-Russian Relations Have Not Yet Been Stabilized Unfortunately, our hope to enhance diplomatic relations with major powers has not been fully realized for Britain. Soviet-British relations are still unstable, because there are still elements within Britain who dream of a united struggle of capitalism to resist socialist countries. However, we hope that the temporary trade agreement that will be signed this time will make it possible to enhance British-Soviet relations.

Actively Promoting Good Neighborly Policies When Litvinov mentioned the Soviet Union's neighboring countries, he said that the signing of the Non-Aggression Pact and the Convention on the Definition of Aggression has increased mutual trust and understanding between the Soviet Union and Poland. He strongly stated that there is a common interest between the two countries, and this relationship is also a product of common dangers and troubles between the two countries. [If we and Poland do not consciously realize the common nature of these troubles, then those who create these troubles will agitate us to experience them. ] Litvinov also mentioned the Soviet Union's eastern neighbors, saying that the Soviet Union is linked with Persia and Afghanistan by non-aggression pacts. At the same time, Karakhan's trip to Persia has made the Soviet-Persian relationship particularly friendly. Although the Soviet Union and the Little Entente countries do not have normal diplomatic relations, they have signed a convention on the definition of aggression. This convention shows that the signatory countries have the desire to maintain peace in Europe. At the same time, the divergence of opinions with Romania has not yet been resolved, which makes the above-mentioned convention even more important. As for the Soviet Union and Sweden, Denmark, Norway, Austria, Greece, and other countries, they have always maintained normal diplomatic relations and have been improving them. Relations with Spain have been revived.

Sympathy for China's Internal and External Troubles When Litvinov mentioned the restoration of diplomatic relations between the Soviet Union and China, he expressed satisfaction and said that the Soviet Union has accepted the Chinese government's proposal to conclude a non-aggression pact, and the draft of the treaty is being examined by the Chinese government. He expressed regret that China is still being invaded by a foreign enemy and has profound internal strife.

No Hostility Towards the German Nation In concluding his glimpse of the Soviet Union's international status, Litvinov elaborated on the relationship between the Soviet Union and Germany and Japan. Starting with Germany, he said that for ten years, Germany and the Soviet Union have had close relations in economic and political aspects, and both countries have been blessed by this relationship. Until this year, the German side discovered various speeches, statements, and actions that violated previous diplomatic relations, which made diplomatic relations deteriorate. Litvinov asked the audience to recall the existence of the following ideas, that is, guns and knives are the usual road for Germany to expand and develop, and personnel in responsible positions who enslaved the Soviet Union have repeatedly made anti-Soviet Russian suggestions and negotiations, and are becoming more active with the above-mentioned ideological system. At this point, Litvinov reiterated the systematic abuse of Soviet Russian institutions and citizens by the German authorities. Some people have tried to attribute the change in German-Soviet Russian diplomatic relations to the Soviet Union's dissatisfaction with the current regime in Germany. Litvinov strongly refuted the fallacy of this statement. He said, we sympathize with the persecution of German comrades, but we Marxists will never be blamed for letting emotions drive politics, and the world knows that we can maintain good relations with capitalist countries under any government, even fascist governments. German politicians once asked me how Germany would dispel the Soviet Union's doubts about Germany's attitude. I always replied, [Germany must stop what it is doing now, and the German government must notify its subordinates to stop what they are doing now. ] We are willing to maintain the best relations with Germany and other countries. We do not plan to make any expansion in the East or the West. We have no hostility towards the German nation and have no intention of invading their territory and rights. We will never encourage other countries to make such an attempt. We hope that Germany can make the same statement to us, and hope that the facts that occur will not contradict this, and at the same time hope that this kind of statement is not only valid for the present, but also when Germany has greater power to implement its aggressive ideas (this kind of thinking was already promoted before the current leaders of Germany took office and is now being promoted by some people) is also valid. ]

Japan's Provocation is Intolerable When Litvinov mentioned the relationship between the Soviet Union and Japan, he said that this relationship has attracted the attention of the world, because Japan's policy is a rumbling black cloud in the international political world. We have almost no so-called national defense in the Far East. Our trust in Japan has always been such. However, since Japan started its military operations in Manchuria, the situation has changed greatly. Japan has made various empty and unbelievable explanations for this. The Japanese government has formally guaranteed to us that our interests, especially our interests on the Chinese Eastern Railway, will not be harmed. This guarantee has been repeatedly stated, and at the same time, the Japanese army continued to advance until they completely occupied Manchuria and created their so-called [Manchukuo]. At this time, regardless of the above-mentioned permissions, they suddenly exerted their power to destroy our interests, and the business of the railway was interrupted. At that time, the whole world was surprised by our calmness and patience. However, the more calm and patient we were, the more shameless and provocative the behavior of the Japanese authorities in Manchuria became. Because we did not want to be hooked by the provocation, we were willing to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway, only trying to recover the cost of the railway. However, during the negotiations, we have confirmed that Japan does not want to buy this railway, but only wants to obtain the railway as a gift without spending a penny. The Japanese representatives did not use verbal negotiations, but used special methods, relying on the assistance of the police and White Russian criminals in Manchuria to forcibly occupy the railway. The Japanese people claimed that Japan had nothing to do with these illegal actions, and the responsible party should be the [independent] Manchukuo. Litvinov strongly refuted the absurdity of this statement. He said, [When we and the world talk about this kind of independence, we have our own views. ]

Gathering Troops on the Border, Russia is Threatened Litvinov pointed out that Japanese troops are currently heavily concentrated on the Manchurian border, military equipment is being transported, and roads and railways are being built. He continued, [This threat is not only to the Chinese Eastern Railway but also to the Soviet border. Our government has to strengthen our national defense and transport the necessary troops. We do not want war. We do not want to threaten Japan. What we ask is that they can also respect our rights and interests.

A Sincere Intention for Peace Should Have Indication If Japan wants to prove its peaceful intentions, the first step should be to stop the policy of arbitrary police action on the Chinese Eastern Railway and restore our destroyed rights. Then continue to negotiate the commercial price of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The second step should be to conclude a non-aggression pact. We wish to hope that Japan's actions will follow the sensitive advice of enlightened patriots in the country, and should not listen to the advice of military adventurers.

International Disarmament Turns into Military Expansion Litvinov concluded this report by mentioning the disarmament conference. He said that this conference can still be regarded as surviving and can still be revived for some time. [However, this is no longer a disarmament conference, but a conference to reorganize armaments. When people talk about reorganizing armaments on one part and reducing armaments on another part, we are afraid that only the first part of this formula can be implemented, not its second part, because the General Assembly can never let those countries that are using their armaments reduce their disarmament, and they openly threaten to use their armaments on a larger scale in the near future. All countries can not regard the non-aggression pact as waste paper, and we can solemnly negotiate disarmament again. Since we are willing to cooperate with other countries, we must keep in mind that the capitalist countries we are targeting have unstable governments and are constantly changing. At the same time, these countries may be ruled by elements who are prepared to sacrifice national interests.

Increase the Strength of the Red Army to Prepare for Possible Attacks

We will have to go out to defend ourselves at this scene and strengthen and improve the main guarantee of our security, namely the Red Army, the Red Navy, and the Red Air Force, as always, and even more than before. We should keep this in mind, that is, even with our aspirations, the time will come when they will summon us to verify Stalin's statement that we will not lose an inch of land. At that time, not only the Red Army soldiers, but the Red People of our Great Federation will go out to defend every inch of land in the East and West of the Soviet Union. The Soviet People, under the leadership of the Communist Party and Stalin, will be able to guarantee that they have a victory in the military field that is on the same scale as the victory they have already obtained. ] (TASS dispatch, 29th)

Finance: Gold Price Drops Slightly by $3.60

Silver Futures and Spot Prices Both Decline, Previous Rise Proves Fleeting

Favorable News for Silver Prices Triggers Reversal and Weakness

The gold market, due to the approaching year-end, tended to stabilize. However, adverse overseas news made it difficult to sustain. In the morning, overseas silver markets rose in England but remained flat in the U.S., exchange rates dropped slightly, and forward silver prices on the Five Metals Exchange fell between 2.5 and 3.5 percent. London raw gold fell by one penny, and the official U.S. buying price of gold remained unchanged. Stock prices experienced both increases and decreases, U.S. cotton shrank by five points, and U.S. wheat was down by a small amount of two and a half points, which improved sentiment. The initial price for processed silver was $84.50, and Guang Gang (Guangdong merchants) accepted the price, causing it to rise to $6. However, because Datong, Ruixing, and others took advantage of the high price to supply silver, prices flattened again. After the opening, Reuters reported that 18 U.S. senators claimed they supported free and unlimited coinage of bimetallic money (gold and silver), and Senator Heller had issued a notice stating he would propose holding a meeting on a gold-silver ratio, changing the ratio to 1:16, before Congress. Due to these adverse messages about to emerge, the domestic market hardened, and sentiment turned bearish. Traders rushed to sell off their holdings, and Guang Gang also sold, leading to prices becoming unsustainable and gradually declining. Before the midday close, prices even broke the $80 mark, as rumors worsened. The price of smelted silver was also at $1,054. The market situation for the first half of the day is recorded below.

The morning opening was at $684.30, an increase of $1.10 from the previous close. Spot goods opened at $4.20. Exchange rates opened with near-term selling prices of British exchange at 1 shilling, 3 pence, 9375, and U.S. exchange at $33.8125. Yongfeng bought silver bars, pushing the price up to $4.70, but as Qiao Zhifu sought to buy U.S. exchange, the domestic market eased. Reuters news favored silver prices, and Datong, Zhifeng, Yongtongxing, Yongruixing, Hengtai, Yuanmao, Yonghengxing, Qianchangxiang, and others successively sold silver bars, causing prices to fall to $1. It was anticipated that HSBC would quote British exchange flat and U.S. exchange down by 125. Shunli, Yuanmao, Yong and others took advantage of the low prices to buy silver bars, and HSBC also unloaded May U.S. dollars at 3125, lowering the price to $3. However, sentiment remained bearish, and Datong and Shunmao sold silver bars. Shanghai also unloaded March U.S. dollars at 75, pushing the price down to within $2. Later, Yuan Cang, Yongheng, Yu, Shenkang were on the buying side, while Shengda and Datong were selling. This led to a prolonged struggle around $2. When adverse news spread, the domestic market hardened, and Yuanmao found it difficult to advance. Finally, with Hengxing repeatedly supplying and Heng, Yu, Huixiang, Yifeng, Yong and others also selling, prices fell to $78. HSBC unloaded April U.S. dollars at 1875, and Yiyu worked hard to buy, gradually pushing prices back up to over $80. Ruikang and Tianfeng sold off, and after much struggle, the midday close was at $679.60. Spot goods were auctioned at $9.20, rising to around $80 after the market closed. It was observed that the highest price during the half-day was $684.70, and the lowest was $678, a difference of $6.70. The result was a drop of $3.60 compared to the previous close.

The quoted price was due to HSBC Bank reducing its U.S. dollar quotation by 125, to $33.25, making the standard gold price $721.80. According to the closing price, about $42 was withheld, $6 more than the previous close. This month's silver bars were all settled at $725.80, January registration at $689, and February at $680. Morning water replenishment was at $695. The price of smelted silver was $1,054. Trading in the market was sluggish, and out-of-town traders were quiet. Only Dafeng and Heng sold 100 taels to Datong for $1,057. The Hongkou bank sold to Yingfeng Heng for $1,054.50, but trading was not high. Finally, $1,057 was offered by someone who needed it, but there were no sellers. There were 1,841 silver bars remaining for January.

Trading in the market was confusing. In summary, Yiyu, Shenkang, Yuanmao, Yonghengtai, Hongxing, Zhifeng, Yongyuan, Maofu, Fuyu, Hengchangyong, Wanxing, and Shunli were on the buying side. Ruikang, Ruixing, Datong, Yicheng, Chunyuan, Yongyi, Dayongheng, Yu, Yuanchun, Changsheng, Yongfu, Taiheng, Bingxing, Dafa, Yongxiang, and Dahexingyong were on the selling side. Shengda Hengxing Yongfeng Yifengyong were net sellers, while Qianchangxiang and Yuanmaoyong were initially sellers then became buyers. The Dalian merchants and Shunli traded around 1,400, with a net purchase of over 200 silver bars. Wanxing traded a total of over 1,100, with a net purchase of over 300 silver bars. The Guangdong merchants Shengda were initially sellers then became buyers, about 600 bars each. Hengxing purchased over 300 and sold over 400. There were a total of 40,481 February contracts.

As of the previous day, for February silver bars, the long positions included Fuchang and Qianchangxiang with over 5,000 each, Wanxing with over 4,300, Yifengyong with over 3,100, Yuanshengyong and Yuanheng Hongxing Hengyu with over 2,000 each, Zhaofengchang with 1,600, Fuyu with 1,819, Run Changyu with over 1,300, and Ruixing Yiyu with over 1,000, and Shunli Yongfeng with over 900 each. The short positions included Yuanmaoyong with over 6,700, Huixiang with over 2,800, Tianfeng and Dachangxiang Dahengxingyong with over 1,800 or 1,900 each, Bingxing with over 2,300, Changshengyong with 1,400, Shenkang Taifeng Cheng with over 1,200 each, Yuanchun and Hengxing with over 800 each, Dacheng with over 900, and Huiyuan Yuanxingyong and Yongfengcheng with over 700 each. U.S. Congress to Propose Gold-Silver Ratio ###

丨丨 One to Sixteen 丨丨

According to yesterday's foreign wire reports, London large bars rose 125 in the near term and 1875 in the long term. U.S. silver was unchanged, but long-term silver prices contracted by 2.5 percent. The British pound against the U.S. dollar fell by half a point, while the U.S. dollar against the British pound decreased by 375. The British pound against the French franc contracted by 1.9 cents, while the U.S. dollar against the French franc rose by half a point. Although banks unloaded after the opening, the market loosened due to Reuters reports that U.S. Senator Heller would propose a gold-silver ratio of 1:16. Zhengjin unloaded May at 3125, HSBC sold April to Chinese merchants at 1875, HSBC took in May at 3125, HSBC bought Zhengjin at 0625, Zhengjin sold March at 1875, HSBC unloaded Zhengjin at 0625, and Qiao Zhifu sold May to Zhengjin at 3125. Year-End Silver Dollar Transfers Exceptionally Busy

Although yesterday was a Saturday, the market atmosphere was usually calm. However, since this year's New Year's Eve falls on a Sunday, all silver and money transfers that should be handled within the year had to be concluded early yesterday. Therefore, everything was exceptionally complicated. Even routine transfers were hindered by excessive procedures and impossible to investigate immediately. The market price for silver dollar discounts was nine fen in both the morning and afternoon, the same as the previous day, with a head mark and a water charge of two or three fen. In discount ticket transactions, over 4.6 million was transferred in the morning, with over 550,000 in new transactions. Afternoon transactions amounted to over 440,000, and transactions in the small general association were over 60,000. Over 1.2 million in paper money was recovered, and over 1.4 million was issued. Silver mortgage transactions amounted to over 1.4 million, with a customer source of 500,000 and an outflow of 300,000. The silver dollar public document transfers from money shops were over 5.1 million, and remittances from various sources were over 700,000. The silver dollar head mark transactions were also impossible to investigate, with over 1 million received in cash. Securities: February Public Bonds Launched Yesterday

The Market Initially Rises Then Falls

Many Bulls Exit the Market

Resulting in a General Decline

Yesterday, the February futures of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange started trading. In the morning, all except the "18 Customs" bonds opened successively. The market was quite favorable, and trends varied due to slight shifts between long and short positions, with both increases and decreases. "Troop Reduction" bonds increased by another three jiao due to continued demand. "Salt Tax" bonds also saw a slight increase. "Gold Long" bonds surged by as much as nine and a half jiao. The remaining bonds saw smaller increases of two or three jiao. In the secondary session, guest merchants and "No. 21" bonds both experienced selling, and market prices gradually turned sluggish, with a general decline of one or two jiao to six or seven jiao. In the afternoon, rumors surfaced, and it was said that "1922 Customs Treasury Bonds" would be auctioned starting January 4, 1923, causing a surge in selling. "Troop Reduction" and "19 Customs" bonds plummeted by one yuan. Later, with Northern merchants covering their short positions, the market stabilized, but still declined by three or four jiao. At the close, only a few transactions were settled, and the market was extremely stable, with prices mostly fluctuating by only one or two jiao. As a result, prices declined by four or five jiao to 1.2 yuan. It was noted that yesterday was the last day of 1922, and there would be a four-day holiday for the New Year and the weekend. Therefore, most floating long and short positions were settled to avoid the risks of a four-day break. Given the unpredictable political situation, many bulls exited the market at the end of the year. The total trading volume was 22.33 million yuan. There were no spot transactions. Futures trading, including salt tax, totaled 7,965,000 yuan, with "Troop Reduction" bonds accounting for 5,570,000 yuan, "1 Yuan Customs Surtax" for 1,475,000 yuan, "20 Coupon 20 Customs" for 3,650,000 yuan, and "Gold Short Gold Long" for 1,390,000 yuan. The remaining transactions ranged from tens of thousands to over a million yuan.

In addition, the stock market will be closed for three days for the New Year holiday on the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of the New Year.

Shanghai's Wheat Market - Central

Southerners eat rice, Northerners eat wheat. In the southern market, wheat is a type of miscellaneous grain, not comparable to rice. In the last ten years or so, southern wheat, especially Shanghai wheat, has occupied an important position in food consumption. This is the result of the development of the mechanized flour industry and a testament to changing tastes.

Before 1921, wheat was generally able to meet the demand with minor imports. But things changed drastically from 1922 onward. In the most recent two years, 22 million dan were imported in 1931, and 15 million dan in 1932. These are the import quantities for the entire country, but most of it was sold in Shanghai. Thus, Shanghai has a close relationship with foreign wheat.

The demand for large quantities of foreign wheat in Shanghai is due to the flour milling industry in the Shanghai area (including Wuxi) being the largest in the country. In order to ensure the color and quantity of the flour, the flour mills must use more foreign wheat. In addition, the decline in the quality of domestic wheat and the reduction in production have further created opportunities for foreign wheat sales. A comparative observation of the table below clearly demonstrates the relationship between foreign wheat and Shanghai. (Unit: 1,000 dan)

Total National Imports Shanghai Imports

1922 873 831

1923 2,595 2,212

1924 5,145 4,663

1925 700 587

1927 1,690 1,646

1928 903 789

1929 5,663 5,464

1930 2,762 2,391

1931 22,773 19,419

1932 15,084 11,021

Therefore, Shanghai flour and wheat merchants felt the pinch first when the import tax on wheat was increased. If the tax increase were for the purpose of protecting domestic agricultural products, it would have been something generally desired. However, observing that the government has only issued the order to tax wheat but has not heard of any possibility of tax exemption in the future, it is clear that the tax increase is more focused on revenue generation.

While Shanghai needs large quantities of foreign wheat, it also needs huge amounts of domestic wheat. The source of domestic wheat is from ships coming from the Jiang and Hai regions, and the quantities are recorded in the customs registers. However, the domestic wheat produced in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, as well as the wheat from Anhui and Huai that comes to Shanghai by train, are not included in the customs registers. The following figures are compiled from customs records and are already substantial. If the quantities not covered by the customs records could also be included in the statistics, the amounts would certainly be greater. Silk and Tea: Little Hope for a Turnaround in European and American Silk Markets

(Interior Silkworm Cocoons Transported to Shanghai for Sale) Shanghai silk factories, since the autumn, have experienced stagnant exports and plummeting silk prices, a rare decline in the silk market since its inception. The silk factories are burdened with stockpiles of silk, making it impossible to sustain operations. Many have declared bankruptcy. The Suzhou and Zhejiang silk factory guilds have repeatedly convened meetings, resolving to petition the government to establish a silk industry control association for relief. They have also organized a joint sales office to investigate silk inventories and cocoon quantities in various ports in order to find ways to promote sales. Shanghai's silkworm cocoon inventory was originally only 54,614 dan. However, because interior merchants transported dry cocoons stored in Wuxi and other ports to Shanghai for sale, Shanghai's silkworm cocoon inventory increased by 802 dan, bringing the total to 55,416 dan.

(Zhejiang Filature Dry Silk Exports to America Remain Stagnant) Zhejiang filature exports to America have been stagnant for a long time, and there has been no turnaround in sales since winter. In the past ten days, only ten bales of white dry silk were shipped to New York via U.S. mail.

(Artificial Silk Sales Clear Before Year-End) As the year-end approaches in the local artificial silk market, customer sales are clearing, and prices are also weakening.
